https://www.istqb.org/documents/ISTQB%20CTFL-PT%20Syllabus%202018%20GA.pdf

Endurance testing focuses on the stability of the system over a time frame specific to the system‚Äôs operational context. This type of testing verifies that there are no resource capacity problems (e.g., memory leaks, database connections, thread pools) that may eventually degrade performance and/or cause failures at breaking points.
